GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A + c3*_t*sin(log(A + c4))

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT numerical expression:** `-0.6789593965981179*A**2 - 0.6789593965981179*A + 0.1640697849676163*sin(log(A + 1))`

Key observations about GT:
- It has an `A²` term with coefficient ≈ -0.6790
- It has an `A` term with coefficient ≈ -0.6790
- It has a `sin(log(A + 1))` term with coefficient ≈ 0.1641
- No explicit `t` dependence (the `_t` was absorbed into `c3`)
- No constant term (when A=0: `sin(log(1))` = `sin(0)` = 0)

The GT contains `sin(log(A+1))` which is a very specific transcendental function. For a candidate to match, it must be able to reproduce this term exactly. Let me check each candidate:

**Candidates 1, 2, 47:** These contain `log(A²*c8 + 1)` terms and `Max(0,A)` terms. Since A≥0, Max(0,A)=A. But `log(A²*c + 1)` is NOT `sin(log(A+1))`. These are fundamentally different basis functions. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 3, 4:** Pure polynomials in A. Cannot produce `sin(log(A+1))`. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 5:** Has `c1*tanh(c2*t + c3) + c4*cos(c5*exp(A*c6))`. The tanh term can be made constant by setting c2=0. The `cos(exp(A*c6))` is not `sin(log(A+1))`. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 6, 7, 8, 9, 10, 11, 14:** These are polynomials in A with exp(t) terms. Setting exp(t) coefficient to 0 leaves polynomials. Cannot produce `sin(log(A+1))`. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 12:** Has `Max(0,A)/(c5*Max(0,A)+1)` = `A/(c5*A+1)`. This is rational, not transcendental. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 13:** `A²*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + c3 + c4*sin(c5*(A+c6)^c7 + c8)`. Setting c1+c2 to match the A coefficient, c3=0. The sin term: `sin(c5*(A+c6)^c7 + c8)`. If c7=0, this becomes sin of a constant. If c5=1, c6=1, c7=0... we need `sin(log(A+1))`. Can `c5*(A+c6)^c7 + c8 = log(A+1)`? The expression `(A+c6)^c7` is a power function, not a logarithm. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 15-50:** Let me scan for any that contain `sin(log(...))`:
- None of them contain `sin(log(...))` explicitly.
- Candidate 28: `c2*tanh(...) + c5*cos(c6*exp(A*c7))` - not matching.
- Candidate 35: `sin(c7*t + c8)` and `log(c6*|A|+1)` - these are multiplied differently, `log(...)*sin(t...)`. If c7=0, this becomes `log(c6*A+1)*sin(c8)` which is `const*log(c6*A+1)`, not `sin(log(A+1))`. **[NO MATCH]**
- Candidate 38: `c5*log(c6*|A*c7|^c8 + 1)` - this is a log, not sin(log). **[NO MATCH]**
- Candidate 49: `c7*log(c8*exp(A*c9)+1)` - this is a softplus-like function, not sin(log). **[NO MATCH]**

None of the candidates contain the basis function `sin(log(A+1))` or any equivalent form.

Going through all 50 candidates systematically, none can produce the `sin(log(A+1))` term that appears in the GT.
